Nh\u01b0ng n\u1ebfu th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng, b\u1ea1n \u0111\u00e3 c\u00f3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \u201cc\u1ed7 m\u00e1y in ti\u1ec1n\" cho ch\u00ednh b\u1ea3n th\u00e2n m\u00ecnh.\n\u2705B (business owner): m\u1ed7i s\u00e1ng khi th\u1ee9c d\u1eady b\u1ea1n ph\u1ea3i suy ngh\u0129 \u0111\u1ebfn th\u1eddi gian, \u00e1p l\u1ef1c, \u0111\u00e1nh \u0111\u1ed1i nhi\u1ec1u th\u1ee9 \u0111\u1ec3 duy tr\u00ec doanh nghi\u1ec7p. V\u00ec l\u00fac n\u00e0y doanh nghi\u1ec7p b\u1ea1n \u0111\u00e3 l\u1edbn, b\u1ea1n ph\u1ea3i qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd nh\u00e2n vi\u00ean t\u1eeb h\u00e0ng tr\u0103m \u0111\u1ebfn h\u00e0ng ng\u00e0n n\u00ean chuy\u1ec7n \u0111\u00f3 c\u0169ng kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n => b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 s\u1eb5n s\u00e0ng tr\u1ea3 gi\u00e1 th\u1eddi gian \u0111\u1ea7u \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ebfn cu\u1ed1i \u0111\u1eddi b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c c\u1ed7 m\u00e1y in ti\u1ec1n l\u1edbn \u0111\u1ec3 nu\u00f4i gia \u0111\u00ecnh c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n?\n\u2705I (investor): \u0111\u00e1nh \u0111\u1ed5i th\u1eddi gian v\u00e0 v\u1ed1n. \u0110\u00e1nh \u0111\u1ed5i th\u1eddi gian \u0111\u1ec3 h\u1ecdc, research, update th\u00f4ng tin, b\u00e1o c\u00e1o t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh, l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn c\u1ee7a doanh nghi\u1ec7p m\u00ecnh \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 h\u00e0ng ng\u00e0y\u2026 \u0111\u1ec3 xem c\u00f3 n\u00ean \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 v\u00e0o doanh nghi\u1ec7p \u0111\u00f3 n\u1eefa kh\u00f4ng? N\u1ebfu n\u00f3 g\u1eb7p bi\u1ebfn c\u1ed1 th\u00ec ph\u1ea3i x\u1eed l\u00fd ti\u1ec1n c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh nh\u01b0 n\u00e0o? Nh\u01b0ng khi \u0111\u00e3 th\u00e0nh nh\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 l\u00e3o luy\u1ec7n, b\u1ea1n s\u1ebd c\u00f3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c nh\u1eefng k\u1ebft qu\u1ea3 x\u1ee9ng \u0111\u00e1ng m\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c qu\u00e1 nhi\u1ec1u.\n\n=> M\u1ed7i l\u0129nh v\u1ef1c trong kim t\u1ee9 \u0111\u1ed3 \u0111\u1ec1u c\u00f3 c\u00e1i gi\u00e1 ph\u1ea3i tr\u1ea3, quan tr\u1ecdng l\u00e0 l\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n mu\u1ed1n cu\u1ed9c s\u1ed1ng c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh s\u1ebd nh\u01b0 th\u1ebf n\u00e0o.\n\nM\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 gi\u1ea3i ph\u00e1p \u0111\u1ec3 d\u1ecbch chuy\u1ec3n kim t\u1ee9 \u0111\u1ed3 hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3\n\ud83c\udf1fB\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 k\u1ebft h\u1ee3p nh\u00f3m E v\u00e0 S. T\u1ef1 m\u1edf c\u00f4ng ty l\u00e0m cho m\u00ecnh xong sau \u0111\u00f3 tr\u00edch l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn m\u1ed7i th\u00e1ng \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0. T\u1ef1 m\u1edf c\u00f4ng ty l\u00e0m cho m\u00ecnh xong sau \u0111\u00f3 tr\u00edch l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn m\u1ed7i th\u00e1ng \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0. L\u00fac n\u00e0y n\u1ebfu l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn cao, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 chia ra \u0111\u1ea7u t\u1ef1 v\u00e0o nhi\u1ec1u t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n kh\u00e1c nhau.\n\ud83c\udf1fK\u1ebft h\u1ee3p E, S, I. Nh\u01b0ng n\u1ebfu c\u00f2n tr\u1ebb th\u00ec ch\u00fang ta n\u00ean th\u1ef1c hi\u1ec7n \u0111i\u1ec1u \u0111\u00f3, v\u00ec n\u1ebfu nh\u01b0 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng m\u00ecnh s\u1ebd ti\u1ebft ki\u1ebfm \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c nhi\u1ec1u kho\u1ea3ng th\u1eddi gian v\u1ec1 sau. Designers from all over the world flocked to Bayern, eager to showcase their latest creations on the fabulous foursome. Whiskers utilized his stealth and cunning, blending into the shadows and carefully stalking his prey. Here are four must-visit attractions in Trang An:\n\nTam C\u1ed1c - B\u00edch \u0110\u1ed9ng: \nTam C\u1ed1c, often referred to as the \"Halong Bay on land,\" is famous for its mesmerizing landscape of limestone karsts and winding waterways. B\u00edch \u0110\u1ed9ng, an ancient Buddhist pagoda, is nestled within the mountains and provides a unique spiritual experience.\n\nCh\u00f9a B\u00e1i \u0110\u00ednh: \nCh\u00f9a B\u00e1i \u0110\u00ednh is one of the largest Buddhist temple complexes in Southeast Asia, and it's an architectural marvel. The temple complex is set against the backdrop of picturesque karst formations, making it an ideal place for both spiritual reflection and admiration of Vietnam's natural beauty. The grandeur of Ch\u00f9a B\u00e1i \u0110\u00ednh, with its intricate details and massive statues, is truly a sight to behold.\n\nL\u00e0ng c\u1ed5 \u0110\u1ed3ng V\u00e2n: \nDong Van Ancient Village is a hidden gem in Trang An, offering a glimpse into the traditional Vietnamese way of life. The village exudes charm with its ancient houses, cobbled streets, and lush gardens. Strolling through the village, you'll feel like you've stepped back in time. It's an excellent place to interact with locals, learn about their customs, and sample traditional Vietnamese dishes.\n\nSu\u1ed1i Ti\u00ean: \nSu\u1ed1i Ti\u00ean, or Fairy Stream, is a pristine natural wonder located in the heart of Trang An. The stream meanders through a lush, jungle-covered valley, offering an enchanting trek along its banks. The clear waters and lush surroundings make it a perfect spot for a refreshing swim. It's a fantastic place for nature lovers and those seeking serenity in the midst of Vietnam's breathtaking landscapes.\n\nTrang An, with its blend of natural splendor and cultural treasures, is a destination that will leave you in awe. Whether you're exploring limestone caves, admiring ancient temples, immersing yourself in traditional village life, or rejuvenating in nature, Trang An promises an unforgettable journey that captivates both the heart and soul.", "replyCount": 12, "retweetCount": 0, "likeCount": 13, "quoteCount": 0, "conversationId": 1714148705702424733, "hashtags": [], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": 108, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": null, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"https://mobile.twitter.com\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter Web App</a>", "sourceUrl": "https://mobile.twitter.com", "sourceLabel": "Twitter Web App", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F8nfzgzXEAEFdFT.png"}, {"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F8nf8YYXkAAc-0U.jpg"}, {"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F8ngJGsW4AAf4YE.png"}, {"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F8ng9QmWUAECckY.jpg"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}
